      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kirsten Simkiss" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kirsten Simkiss" href="/user/show/16550352-kirsten-simkiss">Kirsten Simkiss</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16550352-kirsten-simkiss?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16550352-kirsten-simkiss?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16550352-kirsten-simkiss?shelf=own-paperback">own-paperback</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer509927090" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16635879669433972003">My true rating for this is 4.5 stars, but I'm rating it 5 for Goodread's purposes because it brings the average closer to my true rating for the book.<br/><br/>The last time I read this, I was probably a younger high schooler. It's been A WHILE. For that reason, I was a little apprehensive going into this. I've read more than a few books before where I realized how much nostalgia had colored my view of the book. Fortunately, this seems to be one of those books where my younger brain was very definitely ri</span>
  <span id="freeText16635879669433972003" style="display:none">My true rating for this is 4.5 stars, but I'm rating it 5 for Goodread's purposes because it brings the average closer to my true rating for the book.<br /><br />The last time I read this, I was probably a younger high schooler. It's been A WHILE. For that reason, I was a little apprehensive going into this. I've read more than a few books before where I realized how much nostalgia had colored my view of the book. Fortunately, this seems to be one of those books where my younger brain was very definitely right. This book was a great read. As I said, it had been a while so I remembered the general gist of things, but I really didn't remember much of the specifics of the story. It was really fun experiencing it all again.<br /><br />I do have to say that there were some smaller things I found to be a little juvenile, but nothing that was outright awful. The concept of being stuck in a video game remains utterly fascinating to me. This book absolutely had a formative view of how I view plot-based games. I'm sure one day something like this will cease to be science fiction and we will have games that are virtual reality inserts, but I'm not sure I'll ever see that in this lifetime.<br /><br />I would definitely recommend this book to a friend. It's a great read and I think it's appropriate to all ages.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16635879669433972003" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('hilMObPRC9VF7pRhCDSJx08na6n4oouVP7VlXKa2uK/EfUtDrI9sG+Wyquz5mKI06GML4PRQSPxlT5BvtucmXA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('rRbuA9Vepm5jpobGcHaZH9rb0SyRj2bfClZOeFpwoV/vQul5ygDBoMP6uEuB2rLsfZ+xZZ19pbZQrLtLSiE/rA==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer5279382180490946896">Vivian Vande Velde (born 1951, currently residing in Rochester, New York) is an American author who writes books primarily aimed at young adults.<br/><br/>Her novels and short story collections usually have some element of horror or fantasy, but are primarily humorous. Her book <u>Never Trust a Dead Man</u> (1999) received the 2000 Edgar Award for Best Young Adult Novel. She says that she really likes to write for</span>
  <span id="freeText5279382180490946896" style="display:none">Vivian Vande Velde (born 1951, currently residing in Rochester, New York) is an American author who writes books primarily aimed at young adults.<br /><br />Her novels and short story collections usually have some element of horror or fantasy, but are primarily humorous. Her book <u>Never Trust a Dead Man</u> (1999) received the 2000 Edgar Award for Best Young Adult Novel. She says that she really likes to write for children. She likes to do school talks to children. She does many book conventions and also gives writing classes.<br /><br /></span>
